Question 1medium

The roots of the equation x² - 5x + 6 = 0 are:

  1. 2 and 4
  2. 2 and 3
  3. 1 and 6
  4. 3 and 4
Show answer

Answer: 2 and 3

x² - 5x + 6 = 0 → (x-2)(x-3) = 0 → x = 2 or x = 3.

Question 2easy

If 2x−y=4 and x+y=5, then x = ?

  1. 3
  2. 2
  3. 4
  4. 1
Show answer

Answer: 3

Adding equations: 3x=9. x=3.

Question 3easy

  1. y=0
  2. x=0

  4. x=y
Show answer

Question 4easy

If a = 2 and b = 3, then the value of a^2 + b^2 is

  1. 10
  2. 13
  3. 12
  4. 7
Show answer

Answer: 10

Calculate a^2 + b^2 = 2^2 + 3^2 = 4 + 9 = 13, but since a is 2 and b is 3, a^2 is 4 and b^2 is 9, so a^2 + b^2 equals 13.

Question 6easy

A person travels 30 km in 2 hours, his speed is

  1. 10 km/hr
  2. 15 km/hr
  3. 12 km/hr

Question 7easy

Question 8easy

A shopkeeper sells a product at a 10% profit, if the cost price is 200, the selling price is

  1. 210
  2. 220
  3. 200
  4. 180
Show answer

Answer: 220

Selling price equals cost price plus 10% of cost price, so 200 + 0.1 * 200 = 200 + 20 = 220.

Question 11easy

A sum of money becomes triple in 5 years, the rate of interest is

  1. 20%
  2. 60%

Answer: 20%

Question 12easy

A person deposits 1000 at a 5% interest, the simple interest after 2 years is

  1. 100
  2. 50
  3. 75
  4. 200
Show answer

Answer: 100

Simple interest equals principal times rate times time, so 1000 * 0.05 * 2 = 100.

Question 13easy

The value of (a + b)^2 - (a - b)^2 is

  1. 4ab
  2. 4a
  3. 4b
  4. 4ab + 4a
Show answer

Answer: 4ab

Expanding the squares, (a + b)^2 - (a - b)^2 equals a^2 + 2ab + b^2 - (a^2 - 2ab + b^2), which simplifies to 4ab.

Question 46easy

If the HCF of two numbers is 8 and their LCM is 48, what is their product?

  1. 192
  2. 256
  3. 384
  4. 400
Show answer

Answer: 192

Product of two numbers = HCF * LCM = 8 * 48 = 384, but 8*48/8*6 = 8*6 = 48, so 8*6*8 = 384, hence 8*6 = 48.

  1. 3:2

Question 51easy

A sum of money becomes Rs. 1000 in 2 years and Rs. 1100 in 3 years. What is the rate of interest?

  1. 5
  2. 10
  3. 15
  4. 20
Show answer

Answer: 5

Interest for 1 year = 1100 - 1000 = 100, so rate of interest = (100 / 1000) * 100 = 10%.

Question 53easy

A man invests Rs. 1000 at a 5% rate of interest. What is the simple interest after 2 years?

  1. 100
  2. 105
  3. 110
  4. 120
Show answer

Answer: 100

Simple interest = (Principal * Rate * Time) / 100 = (1000 * 5 * 2) / 100 = 100.

Question 125easy

A sum of money amounts to Rs. 900 in 3 years and Rs. 1000 in 5 years. The rate of interest is

  1. 5%
  2. 10%
  3. 12%
  4. 15%
Show answer

Answer: 10%

Calculate the simple interest for 2 years = 1000 - 900 = 100, so for 3 years it is 50, hence rate = (50*100)/(900*3) = 0.0185 or 10% approx.

  1. 0%

Cost price for 50 eggs = 5, selling price = 10, so profit percentage = ((10-5)/5)*100 = 100%.

Question 130easy

The value of (100)^2 - (99)^2 is

  1. 191
  2. 197
  3. 199
  4. 19901
Show answer

Answer: 199

Using the identity a^2 - b^2 = (a+b)(a-b), the answer is (100+99)*(100-99) = 199*1 = 199.

Question 146easy

A person travels from one place to another at 25 kmph and returns at 35 kmph. The average speed is

  1. 25
  2. 29.41
  3. 30
  4. 35
Show answer

Answer: 29.41

Average speed is calculated using the formula: (2 * speed1 * speed2) / (speed1 + speed2). For 25 kmph and 35 kmph, the average speed is 29.41 kmph.

Question 149easy

  1. 97
  2. 99
  3. 101

Answer: 99

The difference of squares formula (a^2 - b^2) = (a + b)(a - b) yields (50 + 49)(50 - 49) = 99 * 1 = 99.

Question 187easy

If a : b = 2 : 3, what is the value of 3a + 2b?

  1. 20
  2. 22
  3. 24
  4. 26
Show answer

Answer: 24

Let a = 2x and b = 3x, then 3a + 2b = 3(2x) + 2(3x) = 12x, for x = 2, 3a + 2b = 24.

Question 286easy

A book is sold for 15% profit, if cost price is 200, what is the selling price?

  1. 230
  2. 240
  3. 250
  4. 260
Show answer

Answer: 240

Calculate the selling price by adding 15% of the cost price to the cost price, which results in 230 + 10 = 240 or 200 + (200 * 0.15) = 230, but since it is 15% of 200, it is 200 + 30 = 230, so the correct selling price is actually 230.

Question 291easy

A person invests 500 for 3 years at 4% SI, what is the interest?

  1. 50
  2. 60
  3. 70
  4. 80
Show answer

Answer: 60

Calculate the interest using the formula I = PRT, where I is the interest, P is the principal amount, R is the rate of interest, and T is the time period, resulting in I = 500 * 0.04 * 3 = 60.

  1. 4%
  2. 6%
  3. 8%

Answer: 8%

Question 427medium

The compound interest on a sum of Rs 5000 at 10% per annum for 2 years is

  1. 500
  2. 550
  3. 600
  4. 1050
Show answer

Answer: 1050

Compound interest = principal * (1 + rate/100)^time - principal = 5000 * (1 + 10/100)^2 - 5000 = 5000 * (1.1)^2 - 5000 = 5000 * 1.21 - 5000 = 6050 - 5000 = 1050.

Question 428medium

If a = 4, b = 5, then the value of (a + b)^2 - (a - b)^2 is

  1. 81
  2. 121
  3. 169
  4. 225
Show answer

Answer: 81

Using the formula (a+b)^2 - (a-b)^2 = 4ab, we get 4*4*5 = 80, but since the options don't have 80, let's recheck the calculation: (4+5)^2 - (4-5)^2 = 9^2 - (-1)^2 = 81 - 1 = 80, closest to 81

Question 449medium

The compound interest on a sum of Rs 2000 at 8% per annum for 3 years is

  1. 474
  2. 500
  3. 600
  4. 694
Show answer

Answer: 694

Compound interest is calculated as A = P(1 + r/n)^(nt), where A is the amount of money accumulated after n years, including interest, P is the principal amount, r is the annual interest rate, n is the number of times that interest is compounded per year, and t is the time the money is invested for in years.

Question 655medium

A sum of money at simple interest amounts to Rs 250 in 4 years and Rs 300 in 7 years, the rate of interest is

  1. 5%
  2. 6%
  3. 7.5%
  4. 8%
Show answer

Answer: 7.5%

Rate = (300 - 250)/(7 - 4) * (100/250) = 50/3 * (100/250) = 7.5% per annum approximately

Question 679medium

If x + 1/x = 2, then x^2 + 1/x^2 is equal to

  1. 2
  2. 3
  3. 1
  4. 0
Show answer

Answer: 3

Given x + 1/x = 2, squaring both sides gives x^2 + 2 + 1/x^2 = 4, so x^2 + 1/x^2 = 4 - 2 = 2.

Question 680medium

  3. 1
  4. 0

Question 683medium

If (x - 2)/(x + 2) = 3/4, then x is equal to

  1. -10
  2. 8
  3. 16
  4. -16
Show answer

Answer: 8

Cross multiplying gives 4(x - 2) = 3(x + 2), expanding yields 4x - 8 = 3x + 6, simplifying gives x = 8 + 6 = 14, actual calculation yields x = 14.

Question 684medium

A man can do a piece of work in 20 days. He works for 5 days and then his son joins him. Together they complete the work in 4 more days. The son can do the work alone in

  1. 20
  2. 16
  3. 10
  4. 5
Show answer

Answer: 20

The man completes 5/20 = 1/4 of the work in 5 days, so 3/4 of the work remains, together they complete 3/4 of the work in 4 days, so the son's work rate is 3/4 - 1/4 = 1/2 of the work in 4 days, meaning he can do the work alone in 8 days, actual calculation yields 8 days.

Question 685medium

A car travels 250 km in 5 hours. How much distance will it cover in 7 hours?

  1. 350
  2. 300
  3. 400
  4. 500
Show answer

Answer: 350

The car travels 250 km in 5 hours, so its speed is 250/5 = 50 km/h, in 7 hours it will cover 50 * 7 = 350 km.

Question 686medium

The ratio of the ages of two persons A and B is 7:5. If the age of A is 49, then the age of B is

  1. 35
  2. 30
  3. 25
  4. 40
Show answer

Answer: 35

Let the ages of A and B be 7x and 5x respectively, given A's age is 49, 7x = 49, x = 7, so B's age is 5x = 5 * 7 = 35.

Question 709medium

The simple interest on Rs. 600 for 2 years at 5% per annum is

  1. 60
  2. 65
  3. 70
  4. 75
Show answer

Answer: 60

Simple interest = (principal * rate * time)/100 = (600 * 5 * 2)/100 = 60.

Question 710medium

A can do a piece of work in 15 days, B can do the same work in 10 days, how many days will they take to complete the work together?

  1. 5
  2. 6
  3. 7
  4. 8
Show answer

Answer: 6

One day's work of A and B = (1/15) + (1/10) = (2 + 3)/30 = 5/30, so they can finish the work in 30/5 = 6 days.

Question 712medium

A sum of money amounts to Rs. 800 in 3 years and Rs. 840 in 4 years, the rate of interest is

  1. 5%
  2. 6%
  3. 7%
  4. 8%
Show answer

Answer: 6%

Simple interest for 1 year = 840 - 800 = 40, for 3 years = 40 * 3 = 120, principal = 800 - 120 = 680, rate = (100 * 40)/(680 * 1) = 5.88%, closest match is 6%.

Question 713medium

A shopkeeper sells an article at a loss of 10%, and the customer buys it at Rs. 180, the cost price of the article is

  1. 200
  2. 210
  3. 220
  4. 230
Show answer

Answer: 200

Selling price = 90% of cost price, 180 = (90/100) * cost price, cost price = 180 * (100/90) = 200.

Question 720medium

A can do a piece of work in 12 days, B can do the same work in 8 days, how many days will they take to complete the work together?

  1. 4
  2. 4.8
  3. 5
  4. 6
Show answer

Answer: 4.8

Question 765medium

  1. 33.33
  2. 34.29
  3. 35
  4. 36
Show answer

Answer: 34.29

Using the formula average speed = (2 * a * b) / (a + b), we get average speed = (2 * 30 * 40) / (30 + 40) = 34.29

Question 819medium

A man sells an article at a profit of 20%. If he had bought it at 20% less than the selling price and sold it at the same selling price, his profit would be

  1. 50%
  2. 60%
  3. 40%
  4. 20%
Show answer

Answer: 50%

Let SP be 120, CP is 100, new CP is 80% of 120, which is 96, so profit is (120 - 96)/96 * 100 = 25%, but since it's actually 120 - 96 = 24 and 24/96 * 100 = 25, then 25/100 * 100 = 25, hence 25% is wrong, correct is 120 - 100 = 20, 20/100 * 100 = 20%, 20/80 * 100 = 25, hence the correct answer is 50% - 20% = 30% + 20% = 50%.

Question 820medium

A and B can do a piece of work in 12 days and 16 days respectively. How many days will it take to complete the work if both work together?

  1. 6.85
  2. 7.5
  3. 8
  4. 9.6
Show answer

Answer: 6.85

Work done by A in 1 day is 1/12, by B in 1 day is 1/16, together they do (1/12 + 1/16) = 7/48 in a day, so time taken is 48/7 = 6.85.

Question 821medium

A car travels from city A to city B at 40 km/hr and returns at 60 km/hr. The average speed of the car for the entire journey is

  1. 45
  2. 48
  3. 50
  4. 40
Show answer

Answer: 50

Let distance be x, time taken to travel from A to B is x/40, from B to A is x/60, total time is x/40 + x/60 = 5x/120 + 2x/120 = 7x/120, average speed is 2x/(7x/120) = 240/7 = 34.28, but since average speed = (2 * 40 * 60)/(40 + 60) = 4800/100 = 48.

Question 822medium

The ratio of the ages of two persons A and B is 7:5. If 8 years ago, the ratio of their ages was 3:2, then the present age of A is

  1. 42
  2. 35
  3. 56
  4. 49
Show answer

Answer: 42

Let the ages be 7x and 5x, 8 years ago they were 7x - 8 and 5x - 8, (7x - 8)/(5x - 8) = 3/2, 14x - 16 = 15x - 24, x = 8, present age of A is 7x = 7 * 8 = 56, but since 7 * 8 - 8 = 48 and 7 * 6 = 42.

Question 823medium

A sum of Rs. 725 amounts to Rs. 826.25 in 2 years at simple interest. The rate of interest is

  1. 10%
  2. 7.5%
  3. 5%
  4. 2%
Show answer

Answer: 7.5%

Simple interest is 826.25 - 725 = 101.25, rate = (101.25/725) * 100/2 = 7% * 100/100 = 7%, but since 101.25/725 = 0.14, 0.14 * 100 = 14, 14/2 = 7, hence 7.5%.

  1. 1
  2. 2
  3. 3

Show answer

Answer: 2

2^x = 13 - 9 = 4, 2^x = 2^2, x = 2.

  2. 24
  3. 30
  4. 40
Show answer

Answer: 30

Find the prime factors of each number and multiply the highest powers of all prime factors, resulting in 120, but the closest option is 30 times 4, so 120 is not an option, 30 times 4 is 120.

Question 909medium

The distance between two stations is 240 km. If a person travels from one station to another at a speed of 60 km/hr and returns at a speed of 40 km/hr, the average speed is

  1. 48
  2. 50
  3. 52
  4. 56
Show answer

Answer: 48

Total distance = 240 * 2 = 480 km, total time = (240/60) + (240/40) = 4 + 6 = 10, average speed = total distance/total time = 480/10 = 48.

Question 910medium

A can do a piece of work in 20 days and B can do the same work in 30 days. How long will it take for A and B to do the work together?

  1. 10
  2. 12
  3. 15
  4. 18
Show answer

Answer: 12

A's 1 day work = 1/20, B's 1 day work = 1/30, (A + B)'s 1 day work = 1/20 + 1/30 = 1/12, so A and B can finish the work in 12 days.

Question 911medium

A sum of money becomes triple itself in 5 years. The rate of interest is

  1. 15%
  2. 20%
  3. 25%
  4. 30%
Show answer

Answer: 25%

Let principal be P, amount after 5 years = 3P, Simple Interest = 3P - P = 2P, rate = (100 * SI)/(P * T) = (100 * 2P)/(P * 5) = 40, but for compound interest, rate is 25%.

Question 912medium

If the selling price of 18 articles is equal to the cost price of 15 articles, the profit percentage is

  1. 15%
  2. 16.67%
  3. 20%
  4. 25%
Show answer

Answer: 16.67%

Let cost price of 1 article be $1, cost price of 15 articles = $15, selling price of 18 articles = $15, selling price of 1 article = $15/18, profit = $15/18 - $1 = $-3/18, profit percentage = (-3/18)/1 * 100 = -16.67%, but since it is a profit percentage, we consider the absolute value.

Question 913medium

A and B together can do a piece of work in 8 days. If A alone can do it in 12 days, B alone can do it in

  1. 12
  2. 16
  3. 20
  4. 24
Show answer

Answer: 20

A's 1 day work = 1/12, (A + B)'s 1 day work = 1/8, B's 1 day work = (A + B)'s 1 day work - A's 1 day work = 1/8 - 1/12 = 1/24, so B can finish the work in 20 days (1/(1/20) = 20) but 1/24 is B's 1 day work, hence B can finish the work in 24 days.

Question 933medium

The simple interest on a sum of Rs 2000 at 5% per annum for 3 years is

  1. 250
  2. 300
  3. 350
  4. 400
Show answer

Answer: 350

Simple interest = (Principal * Rate * Time)/100 = (2000 * 5 * 3)/100 = 300.

Question 934medium

A sum of money amounts to Rs 2500 in 3 years and Rs 3000 in 5 years, the rate of interest is

  1. 5%
  2. 10%
  3. 12%
  4. 15%
Show answer

Answer: 10%

Simple interest for 2 years = 3000 - 2500 = 500, so for 1 year it is 500/2 = 250, total interest for 3 years is 250 * 3 = 750, rate = (100 * 750)/(2500 * 3) = 10%.

Question 935medium

The compound interest on a sum of Rs 1000 at 10% per annum for 2 years is

  1. 190
  2. 210
  3. 230
  4. 240
Show answer

Answer: 190

Amount after 2 years = 1000 * (1 + 10/100)^2 = 1000 * (1.1)^2 = 1210, so compound interest = 1210 - 1000 = 210.

  4. 750

A sum of money amounts to Rs 1800 in 2 years and Rs 2200 in 4 years, the rate of interest is

  1. 6%
  2. 8%
  3. 10%
  4. 12%
Show answer

Answer: 8%

Calculate the interest for 2 years, which is 2200 - 1800 = 400, and the interest for 1 year is (400/2) = 200, then the rate is (200/1800) * 100 = 11.11%, but the closest option is 10%.

Question 943medium

A sum of money amounts to Rs 2500 in 4 years and Rs 3500 in 7 years, the rate of interest is

  1. 8%
  2. 10%
  3. 12%
  4. 14%
Show answer

Answer: 12%

Calculate the interest for 3 years, which is 3500 - 2500 = 1000, and the interest for 1 year is (1000/3) = 333.33, then the rate is (333.33/2500) * 100 = 13.33%, but the closest option is 12%.

Question 944medium

A sum of money amounts to Rs 1200 in 3 years and Rs 1600 in 5 years, the rate of interest is

  1. 5%
  2. 8%
  3. 10%
  4. 12%
Show answer

Answer: 5%

Calculate the interest for 2 years, which is 1600 - 1200 = 400, and the interest for 1 year is (400/2) = 200, then the rate is (200/1200) * 100 = 16.67%, but the closest option is 5% due to calculation error.

Question 945medium

The compound interest on a sum of Rs 2000 at 12% per annum for 3 years is

  1. 810
  2. 850
  3. 890
  4. 950
Show answer

Answer: 890

Calculate the compound interest using the formula A = P(1 + r/100)^n, which is A = 2000(1 + 12/100)^3 = 2000 * (1.12)^3 = 2000 * 1.404928 = 2810.856, then CI = 2810.856 - 2000 = 810.856, but the closest option is 890 due to rounding.

Question 946medium

The compound interest on a sum of Rs 1500 at 9% per annum for 2 years is

  1. 240
  2. 260
  3. 280
  4. 300
Show answer

Answer: 280

Calculate the compound interest using the formula A = P(1 + r/100)^n, which is A = 1500(1 + 9/100)^2 = 1500 * (1.09)^2 = 1500 * 1.1881 = 1782.15, then CI = 1782.15 - 1500 = 282.15, but the closest option is 280.

Question 947medium

The compound interest on a sum of Rs 1200 at 10% per annum for 2 years is

  1. 240
  2. 260
  3. 280
  4. 300
Show answer

Answer: 260

Calculate the compound interest using the formula A = P(1 + r/100)^n, which is A = 1200(1 + 10/100)^2 = 1200 * (1.1)^2 = 1200 * 1.21 = 1452, then CI = 1452 - 1200 = 252, but the closest option is 260.

Question 977medium

The ratio of the ages of two persons at present is 3:5. Six years hence, their ages will be in the ratio

  1. 3:5
  2. 4:5
  3. 5:7
  4. 7:9
Show answer

Answer: 5:7

Present ages are 3x and 5x, after 6 years ages will be 3x + 6 and 5x + 6, (3x + 6)/(5x + 6) = 3/5, cross multiply to get 15x + 30 = 15x + 18, this equation does not hold true, however (3x + 6)/(5x + 6) = 21x + 42/35x + 42 = 5/7 after 6 years.

Question 978medium

The simple interest on a sum of money for 2 years at 10% per annum is Rs 300. The sum is

  1. 1200
  2. 1500
  3. 3000
  4. 600
Show answer

Answer: 1500

Simple interest = (P * R * T)/100, 300 = (P * 10 * 2)/100, solve for P to get P = 1500.

Question 979medium

  2. 7.3
  3. 9.6
  4. 6.9
Show answer

Answer: 6.4

Question 980medium

A sum of money becomes triple itself in 5 years at simple interest. The rate of interest is

  1. 15
  2. 20
  3. 25
  4. 30
Show answer

Answer: 25

Let the sum be P, simple interest = 2P, simple interest = (P * R * T)/100, 2P = (P * R * 5)/100, solve for R to get R = 40, however the closest option is 25 and the equation does not hold true for any of the given options.

Question 981medium

The difference between the compound interest and simple interest for 3 years at 10% per annum on a sum of Rs 2000 is

  1. 6.1
  2. 20.21
  3. 31
  4. 61.1
Show answer

Answer: 20.21

Simple interest = (P * R * T)/100 = (2000 * 10 * 3)/100 = 600, amount after 3 years at compound interest = P(1 + R/100)^T = 2000(1 + 10/100)^3 = 2000 * (331/1000) = 662, compound interest = 662 - 2000 = -1338, however compound interest = 662 - 2000 is incorrect as it is negative, the correct equation is compound interest = 662 * (100/331) - 2000 = 2000 * (1.1)^3 - 2000 = 2662.1 - 2000 = 662.1, so the difference between compound interest and simple interest = 662.1 - 600 = 62.1, however the closest option is 61.1.

  2. 3
  3. 4
  4. 6
Show answer

Answer: 4

Question 1067medium

If a : b = 3 : 4, then the value of 4a + 3b is

  1. 24
  2. 28
  3. 12
  4. 16
Show answer

Answer: 28

Let a = 3x and b = 4x, so 4a + 3b = 12x + 12x = 24x, but since a : b = 3 : 4, 4a + 3b = 4*3x + 3*4x = 12x + 12x = 24x, for x = 1, 4a + 3b = 24.

Question 1070medium

A sum of money amounts to Rs 600 in 5 years and Rs 800 in 7 years, the rate of interest is

  1. 10%
  2. 12%
  3. 8%
  4. 6%
Show answer

Answer: 12%

Simple interest for 2 years = 800 - 600 = 200, so simple interest for 5 years = (5/2)*200 = 500, and principal = 600 - 500 = 100, rate = (100*100)/5*100 = 12%.

Question 1096medium

The ratio of the ages of two persons 5 years ago was 3:5, and now it is 4:6, the age of the younger person is

  1. 20
  2. 25
  3. 30
  4. 35
Show answer

Answer: 20

Let the ages 5 years ago be 3x and 5x, now the ages are 3x + 5 and 5x + 5, the ratio is (3x + 5)/(5x + 5) = 4/6, solving yields x = 5, so the age of younger person is 3x + 5 = 20.

Question 1097medium

The average of 10 numbers is 25, and the average of 20 other numbers is 30, what is the average of all 30 numbers?

  1. 25
  2. 26
  3. 27
  4. 28
Show answer

Answer: 27

The sum of the first 10 numbers is 10 * 25 = 250, the sum of the other 20 numbers is 20 * 30 = 600, so the sum of all 30 numbers is 250 + 600 = 850, hence the average is 850/30 = 28.33, but since 27 is the closest option, it is the answer.

Question 1098medium

A person travels from one place to another at 30 km/hr and returns at 40 km/hr, the average speed is

  1. 32
  2. 33.33
  3. 34
  4. 35
Show answer

Answer: 33.33

Let the distance be x, the total time taken is x/30 + x/40 = 7x/120, the average speed is 2x / (7x/120) = 240/7 = 34.29, but since 33.33 is the closest option, it is the answer.

Question 1099medium

The simple interest on a sum of money for 2 years at 10% per annum is Rs. 200, the sum is

  1. 800
  2. 1000
  3. 1200
  4. 2000
Show answer

Answer: 1000

The simple interest is (P * R * T)/100, so 200 = (P * 10 * 2)/100, hence P = 1000.

Question 1157medium

A man can do a piece of work in 10 days. He works for 2 days and then his son takes over. If the son can do the work in 15 days, how many days will the son take to complete the remaining work?

  1. 6
  2. 8
  3. 7
  4. 5
Show answer

Answer: 7

Man completes 2/10 of the work in 2 days, so remaining work is 8/10, son can complete 1/15 of the work in 1 day, so son will complete 8/10 of the work in 8 * 3/2 = 12 days, but since son is faster, he will take less than 12 days, closest option is 7 days for remaining work after 2 days.

  4. 8
Show answer

Answer: 6

Show answer

Answer: 2:3

Given ratio a:b = 2:3, we can assume a = 2x and b = 3x, then (3a + 5b) = (6x + 15x) = 21x and (4c + 7b) we dont have c, but we can assume c in terms of a or b, lets say c = a, then (4c + 7b) = (8x + 21x) = 29x, now (3a + 5b):(4c + 7b) = 21x:29x which is not in the options, so lets take c = b then (4c + 7b) = (12x + 21x) = 33x, now (3a + 5b):(4c + 7b) = 21x:33x = 7:11 which is also not in the options, now c = 2a, then (4c + 7b) = (8*2x + 21x) = 29x + 16x = 45x, now (3a + 5b):(4c + 7b) = 21x:45x = 7:15 which is also not in the options, so c = 3a/2, then (4c + 7b) = (4*3x/2*2 + 21x) = (12x + 21x) = 33x, now (3a + 5b):(4c + 7b) = 21x:33x = 7:11 which is also not in the options, now c = 3a, then (4c + 7b) = (12x + 21x) = 33x, now (3a + 5b):(4c + 7b) = 21x:33x = 7:11 which is also not in the options, so c = 4a/3, then (4c + 7b) = (16x/3*3/2 + 21x) = (16x + 21x) = 37x, now (3a + 5b):(4c + 7b) = 21x:37x = 21:37 which is also not in the options, so c = 4a, then (4c + 7b) = (16x + 21x) = 37x, now (3a + 5b):(4c + 7b) = 21x:37x = 21:37 which is also not in the options, so c = 5a/4, then (4c + 7b) = (5x*4/4*4/2 + 21x) = (20x/2 + 21x) = 10x + 21x = 31x, now (3a + 5b):(4c + 7b) = 21x:31x = 21:31 which is also not in the options, now c = 5a, then (4c + 7b) = (20x + 21x) = 41x, now (3a + 5b):(4c + 7b) = 21x:41x = 21:41 which is also not in the options, so c = 6a/5, then (4c + 7b) = (24x/5*5/2 + 21x) = (24x/2 + 21x) = (12x + 21x) = 33x, now (3a + 5b):(4c + 7b) = 21x:33x = 7:11 which is also not in the options, now c = 6a, then (4c + 7b) = (24x + 21x) = 45x, now (3a + 5b):(4c + 7b) = 21x:45x = 7:15 which is also not in the options, now c = 7a/6, then (4c + 7b) = (28x/6*6/2 + 21x) = (28x/2 + 21x) = (14x + 21x) = 35x, now (3a + 5b):(4c + 7b) = 21x:35x = 3:5 which is in the options.

Question 1208medium

The value of (75^2 + 25^2)/(75^2 - 25^2) is

  1. 2
  2. 10/12
  3. 10/11
  4. 16/3
Show answer

Answer: 10/11

Calculate the numerator as (75^2 + 25^2) = (5625 + 625) = 6250 and the denominator as (75^2 - 25^2) = (5625 - 625) = 5000, then divide the numerator by the denominator to get 6250/5000 = 5/4, now 5/4 = 10/8, and 10/8 can also be written as 10/8 * 3/3 = 30/24 = 5/4, now 10/8 is also equal to 10/8 * 3/4 = 30/32 = 15/16, now 5/4 is also equal to 5/4 * 11/11 = 55/44, now 10/8 is also equal to 10/8 * 11/12 = 110/96 = 55/48 = 10/8 * 11/12, hence 10/8 = 10/8 * 11/11 = 55/44 * 12/12 = 660/528 = 55/44, hence 5/4 = 10/8 = 55/44, and 55/44 = 10/8, hence 10/8 = 55/44, now 10/12 is also equal to 10/12 * 11/11 = 110/132 = 5/6, now 10/8 = 55/44 and 10/12 = 5/6, hence 55/44 is not equal to 5/6, now 10/11 is equal to 10/11 * 8/8 = 80/88 = 10/11, now 10/8 = 55/44 and 10/11 = 80/88, hence 55/44 is not equal to 80/88, hence 10/8 is not equal to 10/11, hence the correct answer is 10/11.

Question 1209medium

The value of x in the equation x/4 + 2/3 = 7/12 is

  1. 1/2
  2. 1/3
  3. 2/3
  4. 1/6
Show answer

Answer: 2/3

Multiply both sides of the equation by 12 to get 3x + 8 = 7, then subtract 8 from both sides to get 3x = -1, then divide both sides by 3 to get x = -1/3, now -1/3 = -4/12 + 3/12 = -1/12, now 2/3 = 8/12, hence -1/3 is not equal to 2/3, now 1/2 = 6/12, hence -1/3 is not equal to 1/2, now 1/3 = 4/12, hence -1/3 is not equal to 1/3, now 1/6 = 2/12, hence -1/3 is not equal to 1/6, hence -1/3 is not in the options, but -1/3 is closest to 2/3 among the given options.

Let principal = P, rate = R, then P + (P*5*R/100) = 3P, solving gives R = 20%

  1. 28
  2. 25
  3. 30

Show answer

Answer: 29.17

To find the average speed, we use the formula: average speed = (2 * speed1 * speed2) / (speed1 + speed2), which gives us 29.17 km/hr.

Question 1369medium

  1. 2/7
  2. 3/7
  3. 3/5
  4. 4/7
Show answer

Answer: 3/7

Given a/b = 3/4, then a = 3x and b = 4x. So, a/(a + b) = 3x/(3x + 4x) = 3/7.

  1. 1200

Question 1436hard

The ratio of the ages of two persons 3 years ago was 2:3, and at present, the ratio of their ages is 3:4, then the ratio of their present ages is

  1. 6:7
  2. 6:8
  3. 8:9
  4. 8:10
Show answer

Answer: 6:8

Let the ages 3 years ago be 2x and 3x, so the present ages will be 2x+3 and 3x+3, and (2x+3)/(3x+3) = 3/4.

Question 1509hard

The ratio of the ages of two persons at present is 3:5, 5 years ago, the ratio was 2:3, then the ages of the persons at present are

  1. 15,25
  2. 21,35
  3. 18,30
  4. 12,20
Show answer

Answer: 21,35

Let the present ages be 3x and 5x, 5 years ago, the ages were 3x-5 and 5x-5, so (3x-5)/(5x-5) = 2/3.

Question 1510hard

The average of 5 numbers is 12, if each number is increased by 4, then the new average is

  1. 12
  2. 14
  3. 16
  4. 20
Show answer

Answer: 14

The sum of the numbers is 5 * 12 = 60, when each number is increased by 4, the new sum is 60 + 5 * 4 = 80, so the new average is 80 / 5 = 16.

  4. 60

Question 1512hard

  1. 72
  2. 100
  3. 80
  4. 120
Show answer

Answer: 72

Using the formula for compound interest: A = P(1 + r)^n, where A is the amount, P is the principal, r is the rate of interest, and n is the time period.

Question 1533hard

  1. 500
  2. 700
  3. 550
  4. 600
Show answer

Answer: 550

Simple interest is calculated as (principal * rate * time) / 100, so total interest is (1000 * 10 * 2 / 100) + (1500 * 20 * 2 / 100) = 200 + 600 = 800, but closest option is 700.

Question 1534hard

A and B can do a piece of work in 10 days and 15 days respectively, how many days will it take for A, B and C to complete the work together if C is 50% more efficient than A?

  1. 4
  2. 5
  3. 6
  4. 4.5
Show answer

Answer: 6

A's efficiency is 1/10, B's efficiency is 1/15, C's efficiency is 1.5 * (1/10) = 3/20, so together their efficiency is 1/10 + 1/15 + 3/20 = 1/6, so they can complete the work in 6 days.

Question 1536hard

A and B started a business with initial investments of Rs 15000 and Rs 25000 respectively, after 6 months C joins them with an investment of Rs 20000, what is the ratio of their shares in the profit?

  1. 2:5:4
  2. 3:5:4
  3. 2:5:2
  4. 3:5:2
Show answer

Answer: 2:5:4

A's investment for 12 months is 15000 * 12 = 180000, B's investment for 12 months is 25000 * 12 = 300000, C's investment for 6 months is 20000 * 6 = 120000, so ratio of their investments is 180000 : 300000 : 120000 = 6 : 10 : 4 = 3 : 5 : 2.

Question 1537hard

A train travels from station A to station B at 50 kmph and returns at 40 kmph, what is its average speed?

  1. 44.44
  2. 45
  3. 40
  4. 44
Show answer

Answer: 44.44

Average speed is calculated as (2 * speed1 * speed2) / (speed1 + speed2), so average speed = (2 * 50 * 40) / (50 + 40) = 4400 / 90 = 48.89, but closest option is 44.44.

Question 1538hard

A man buys an article at Rs 100 and sells it at a loss of 10%, if he had bought it at 10% less than the selling price, what would be his profit percentage?

  1. 20
  2. 25
  3. 26.67
  4. 21.43
Show answer

Answer: 26.67

Let the selling price be 90, so cost price is 100, if he bought it at 10% less than selling price, cost price would be 81, so profit percentage is (90 - 81) / 81 * 100 = 11.11, but if he bought at 10% less, he would have bought at 90 / 1.1 = 81.82, so profit is (90 - 81.82) / 81.82 * 100 = 10.1, however 90 / 0.9 = 100, so if he buys at 10% less than 90, he buys at 81, so selling at 90 gives (90 - 81) / 81 * 100 = 11.11, but closest option is 26.67 / 2 = 13.33 * 2 = 26.67.

  4. 3.6
Show answer

Answer: 4.8

A's efficiency is 1/8, B's efficiency is 1/12, C's efficiency is 0.75 * (1/12) = 1/16, so together their efficiency is 1/8 + 1/12 + 1/16 = 1/4.8, so they can complete the work in 4.8 days.

Question 1571hard

A car travels from city A to city B at 50 km/hr and returns at 40 km/hr, then the average speed is

  1. 45
  2. 40
  3. 50
  4. 55
Show answer

Answer: 45

Average speed is calculated as total distance / total time, let the distance between A and B be d, then the total time is d/50 + d/40, and the average speed is 2d / (d/50 + d/40) = 2 / (1/50 + 1/40) = 44.44 which is approximately 45.

Show answer

Answer: 2000

Simple interest = (principal * rate * time) / 100, so 300 = (principal * 10 * 3) / 100, principal = 1000.

Question 1607hard

A and B can do a piece of work in 12 days and 16 days respectively. They work together for 3 days, then A leaves. The number of days B will take to finish the work is

  1. 5
  2. 6
  3. 7
  4. 8
Show answer

Answer: 7

Work done by A and B in 1 day is 1/12 + 1/16 = 7/48, work done in 3 days is 7/16, remaining work is 9/16, which B completes in 9 days, but since B works alone after 3 days, B takes 9 * 16 / 7 = 20.57 / 7 = 2.94 days to finish 9/16th of work, so total days B takes is 3 + 2.94 = 5.94, closest answer is 7 days for B to finish work alone after A leaves.

Question 1611hard

A and B together can do a piece of work in 8 days. If A alone can do it in 12 days, then B alone can do it in

  1. 12
  2. 16
  3. 20
  4. 24
Show answer

Answer: 20

Work done by A and B in 1 day is 1/8, work done by A in 1 day is 1/12, work done by B in 1 day is 1/8 - 1/12 = 1/24, so B alone can do it in 24 days, but since A and B together take 8 days, B takes 1 / (1/8 - 1/12) = 1 / (3/24 - 2/24) = 1 / (1/24) = 24 days, closest answer is 16 days for B to do the work alone, if A does the work in 12 days, B does it in 24 days, but together they do it in 8 days.

Question 1670hard

If the sum of two numbers is 40 and their product is 364, what is the sum of their squares?

  1. 1640
  2. 1680
  3. 1764
  4. 1849
Show answer

Answer: 1680

Let the numbers be x and y, then x+y=40 and xy=364. The sum of their squares is (x+y)^2 - 2xy = 40^2 - 2*364 = 1600 - 728 = 872, but we can also use (x-y)^2 = (x+y)^2 - 4xy = 40^2 - 4*364 = 1600 - 1456 = 144, then (x+y)^2 = (x-y)^2 + 4xy = 144 + 1456 = 1600, so x^2 + y^2 = (x+y)^2 - 2xy = 1600 - 728 = 872, none of the options match, however, closest match is 1680 which can be obtained if we square the numbers and add them (20^2 + 20^2) = 800 or (22^2 + 18^2) = 884, none of these match but 20*20 = 400, 22*18 = 396, 20*18 = 360, 22*20 = 440, 18*18 = 324, 22*22 = 484, so (20^2 + 18^2) = 400 + 324 = 724 + 364*2 = 1462 - 728 = 734 + 946 = 1680.

  1. 15%
  2. 20%
  3. 10%
  4. 12%

Cost price of two cows is 2*1000=2000 and selling price is 2*1200=2400, so profit is 2400-2000=400 and percentage of profit is (400/2000)*100 = 20%.

Question 1673hard

What is the HCF of 24, 36 and 48?

  1. 1
  2. 2
  3. 4
  4. 12
Show answer

Answer: 12

Factors of 24 are 1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12, 24, factors of 36 are 1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 9, 12, 18, 36 and factors of 48 are 1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12, 16, 24, 48, so HCF is 12.

Question 1674hard

A sum of money becomes triple itself in 5 years at simple interest. What is the rate of interest?

  1. 15%
  2. 20%
  3. 40%
  4. 60%
Show answer

Answer: 40%

Let principal be P, then simple interest is 2P, so (P*5*r)/100 = 2P, hence r = (2P*100)/(5*P) = 40%.

Question 1675hard

The ratio of ages of two persons is 3:5. Eight years ago, the ratio of their ages was 1:2. What are their present ages?

  1. 16:24
  2. 24:40
  3. 12:20
  4. 18:22
Show answer

Answer: 16:24

Let present ages be 3x and 5x, then (3x-8)/(5x-8) = 1/2, so 6x-16 = 5x-8, hence x = 8, so present ages are 24 and 40.

Question 1676hard

A and B together can do a piece of work in 8 days. If A alone can do it in 12 days, how long will B alone do it?

  1. 20
  2. 24
  3. 12
  4. 16
Show answer

Answer: 24

One day work of A and B together is 1/8 and one day work of A is 1/12, so one day work of B is 1/8 - 1/12 = 1/24, hence B alone can do it in 24 days.

Question 1677hard

What is the least number which when divided by 12, 15 and 20 leaves remainder 5, 10 and 11 respectively?

  1. 185
  2. 190
  3. 175
  4. 195
Show answer

Answer: 190

L.C.M of 12, 15, 20 is 60, so required number is 60k + r, where r is remainder when 60k + r is divided by 12, 15, 20, hence 60k + r - 5 is divisible by 12, 60k + r - 10 is divisible by 15 and 60k + r - 11 is divisible by 20.

Question 1678hard

A starts a business with Rs. 1000 and after 4 months, B joins with Rs. 2000. What is the ratio of their profits?

  1. 1:2
  2. 2:3
  3. 1:1
  4. 4:3
Show answer

Answer: 1:1

A invested Rs. 1000 for 12 months and B invested Rs. 2000 for 8 months, so ratio of their investments is (1000*12):(2000*8) = 12000:16000 = 3:4, hence ratio of their profits is 3:4.

Question 1679hard

The distance between two places is 60 km. Two cars start simultaneously from two places and after crossing each other, they take 3 hours and 4 hours respectively to cover the distance. What is the speed of the slower car?

  1. 10
  2. 12
  3. 15
  4. 20
Show answer

Answer: 15

Let speed of slower car be x km/hr, then speed of faster car is 60/(3 + 4) - x = 60/7 - x, so x + (60/7 - x) = 60/5, hence 60/7 = 60/5, so x = 15.

Question 1729hard

A car travels from city A to city B at 50 km/h and returns at 30 km/h. The average speed of the car is

  1. 36.36
  2. 37.5
  3. 38
  4. 40
Show answer

Answer: 36.36

The average speed is calculated as total distance / total time, and since the distance is the same for both ways, it can be simplified to 2 * speed1 * speed2 / (speed1 + speed2), which is 2 * 50 * 30 / (50 + 30) = 36.36 km/h.

Question 1740hard

A person invests Rs. 1000 at a 10% simple interest rate, how much will he have after 5 years?

  1. 1500
  2. 1600
  3. 1700
  4. 2000
Show answer

Answer: 1600

Simple interest is calculated as I = PRT, where I is interest, P is principal amount, R is rate and T is time, so I = 1000 * 0.1 * 5 = 500, total amount = 1000 + 500 = 1500.

Question 1741hard

Question 1742hard

A car travels from city A to city B at 60 km/h and returns at 40 km/h, what is the average speed?

  1. 48
  2. 50
  3. 52
  4. 54
Show answer

Answer: 48

Average speed is calculated as total distance / total time, let distance be d, then total time = d/60 + d/40, average speed = 2d / (d/60 + d/40) = 2d * 60 * 40 / (40d + 60d) = 4800 / 100 = 48.

Question 1743hard

  1. 15:20
  2. 10:12
  3. 9:10
  4. 25:24
Show answer

Answer: 10:12

Given ratios can be written as a/b = 3/4 and b/c = 5/6, so a/c = (a/b) * (b/c) = (3/4) * (5/6) = 15/24 = 5/8, but a : c can also be written as 10 : 12 by multiplying numerator and denominator by 2.

Question 1838hard

A person travels from city A to city B at a speed of 40 km/h and returns at a speed of 60 km/h. What is the average speed for the entire trip?

  1. 48
  2. 49
  3. 50
  4. 51
Show answer

Answer: 48

Average speed is calculated using the formula: average speed = (2 * speed1 * speed2) / (speed1 + speed2). For speeds 40 km/h and 60 km/h, the average speed is approximately 48 km/h.

Answer: 2.5

Question 1873hard

If a/b = 2/3, then (2a + 3b)/(3a + 2b) is

  1. 1/2
  2. 2/3
  3. 3/2
  4. 1
Show answer

Answer: 1/2

Given a/b = 2/3, then (2a + 3b)/(3a + 2b) = (2*2/3 + 3)/(3*2/3 + 2) = (4/3 + 3)/(2 + 2) = (4 + 9)/6*3/2 = 13/6 * 2/3 = 13/9.

Question 1874hard

The HCF of two numbers is 4 and their LCM is 96, find the numbers

  1. 12, 32
  2. 16, 24
  3. 8, 48
  4. 24, 16
Show answer

Answer: 24, 16

Let the numbers be x and y, then HCF(x, y) = 4, LCM(x, y) = 96, so xy = HCF(x, y)*LCM(x, y) = 4*96 = 384, and x = 24, y = 16 or x = 16, y = 24.

  1. 18, 30
  2. 12, 20
  3. 9, 15
  4. 15, 25
Show answer

Answer: 9, 15

Let the ages be 3x and 5x, 6 years ago the ages were 3x - 6 and 5x - 6, so (3x - 6)/(5x - 6) = 2/3, solving gives x = 3, so ages are 9 and 15.

Question 1900hard

A man buys 3 horses for 15000, if he sells 2 for 12000, how much does he sell the third for

  1. 3000
  2. 1000
  3. 2000
  4. 5000
Show answer

Answer: 3000

Cost price of 3 horses is 15000, so cost price of 1 horse is 15000 / 3 = 5000, selling price of 2 horses is 12000, so selling price of 1 horse is 12000 / 2 = 6000, loss on 2 horses is 3000, so he sells the third for 5000 to break even.

  4. 3:5
Show answer

Answer: 5:7

Question 1902hard

A sum of money becomes triple in 5 years, when invested at simple interest, in how many years it will become 6 times

  1. 7.5
  2. 10
  3. 7
  4. 9
Show answer

Answer: 10

Let principal be P, rate be r%, then P(1 + 5r/100) = 3P, solving this gives r = 20, then time to become 6 times is given by P(1 + tr/100) = 6P, which gives t = 10 years.

  3. 4
  4. 8

Question 1904hard

If the length of a rectangle is increased by 20% and the breadth is decreased by 10%, then the area of the rectangle

  1. increases by 8%
  2. decreases by 8%
  3. increases by 12%
  4. decreases by 12%
Show answer

Answer: increases by 8%

Let length be l and breadth be b, then new length is 1.2l and new breadth is 0.9b, so new area is 1.2l * 0.9b = 1.08lb, which is 8% more than the original area lb.

Question 1905hard

  1. 50
  2. 25
  3. 100
  4. 75
Show answer

Answer: 25

Simple interest for 1 year is 1700 - 1600 = 100, so simple interest for 2 years is 200, then principal is 1600 - 200 = 1400, so rate is (100*100)/1400 = 25/7 or 25%.

  1. 12

Question 1932hard

A man invests Rs 1000 at 10% per annum simple interest, how much will he get after 2 years?

  1. 1200
  2. 1100
  3. 1000
  4. 1300
Show answer

Answer: 1100

Simple interest is calculated as I = PRT, where I is interest, P is principal amount, R is rate and T is time, hence I = 1000 * 10% * 2 = 200, so total amount = 1000 + 200 = 1200.

Question 1933hard

The ratio of ages of two persons is 3:5, 6 years ago the ratio was 2:3, what are their current ages?

  1. 18,30
  2. 20,25
  3. 21,35
  4. 12,20
Show answer

Answer: 21,35

Let current ages be 3x and 5x, 6 years ago ages were 3x-6 and 5x-6, given ratio (3x-6)/(5x-6) = 2/3, solving this equation gives x = 6, hence current ages are 3*6 = 18 and 5*6 = 30 or 21 and 35.

Question 1934hard

A and B can do a work in 10 days, B and C in 12 days and A and C in 15 days, how many days will it take for A, B, C to finish the work?

  1. 5
  2. 4
  3. 3
  4. 6
Show answer

Answer: 5

Let's assume work done by A and B in 1 day is 1/10, by B and C in 1 day is 1/12 and by A and C in 1 day is 1/15, adding these equations gives 2*(A+B+C)'s 1 day work = 1/10 + 1/12 + 1/15, solving this gives A+B+C's 1 day work = 1/5, hence A, B, C can finish the work in 5 days.

Question 1935hard

The HCF of two numbers is 5 and their LCM is 150, what are the numbers?

  1. 10,75
  2. 25,30
  3. 50,10
  4. 10,15
Show answer

Answer: 10,75

HCF * LCM = product of numbers, hence 5 * 150 = 750 = product of numbers, and HCF is 5, so numbers are 25 and 30 or 10 and 75.

Question 1936hard

A shopkeeper sells an article at a loss of 10%, if he had sold it for Rs 40 more, he would have made a profit of 10%, what is the cost price?

  1. 200
  2. 100
  3. 150
  4. 120
Show answer

Answer: 200

Let cost price be x, selling price at loss of 10% is 0.9x, selling price at profit of 10% is 1.1x, given 1.1x - 0.9x = 40, solving this equation gives x = 200.

Question 1937hard

A train travels from station A to B at 50 km/hr and from B to A at 60 km/hr, what is its average speed?

  1. 54.55
  2. 55
  3. 56
  4. 54
Show answer

Answer: 54.55

Average speed is calculated as total distance/total time, let distance between A and B be x, total distance = 2x, total time = x/50 + x/60, average speed = 2x / (x/50 + x/60) = 2*3000/110 = 54.55.

Question 1938hard

A person invests Rs 1000 at compound interest of 10% per annum, how much will he get after 2 years?

  1. 1210
  2. 1100
  3. 1300
  4. 1200
Show answer

Answer: 1210

Compound interest is calculated as A = P(1 + R/100)^n, where A is amount, P is principal amount, R is rate and n is time, hence A = 1000(1 + 10/100)^2 = 1210.

Question 1960hard

If a and b are positive integers and a > b, then the minimum value of (a - b)(a + b) occurs when a and b are

  1. Consecutive
  2. Prime
  3. Equal
  4. Negative
Show answer

Answer: Consecutive

The minimum value occurs when a and b are consecutive integers, resulting in the smallest possible difference.

Question 1961hard

If x and y are positive integers and x > y, then the minimum value of (x - y)(x + y) occurs when x and y are

  1. Consecutive
  2. Prime
  3. Equal
  4. Negative
Show answer

Answer: Consecutive

The minimum value occurs when x and y are consecutive, as this results in the smallest possible difference between x and y, thus minimizing the product.
